401.3(1)*: pa'i skra yon 'dod rdzas rgyan gyis skor gtod la stong nyid bshad nas yon tan bde 
401.4(1)*: dang ldan/ dang po stong 'od gsal byang tsam na/ gtod rigs 'khor bcas stong 
401.5(1)*: nyid stag gsal 'dzin gtod ldan ngo mtshar che/ gtod la ma go ma rtogs ngo mtshar 
401.6(1)*: ce/ sems nyid don la 'jug pa'i sa rtogs go ba bsam/ sems nyid jza bo don 
401.7(1)*: la rtogs par gyis/ gtod la sems nyid don dam jo bo yi/ mtha' bral nang la 
401.8(1)*: spyod pa nzo mtshar che/ sems nyid jo bo stong pa yin/ tig le nyag gcig bon gyi do 
401.9(1)*: bo gcig sems nyid stong pa 'od du gsal ba'i dang / sems nyid ma bcos gsal 
401.10(1)*: stong ngo bo nyid/ sems nyid rig pa rang la 'char ba bon gyi stu/ sems nyid stong 
401.11(1)*: pa'i rig pa ngo bo gsal/ gsal stong 'dzin med bon gyi sems gsal sku/ sku 
401.12(1)*: gsum dza bo nyid gyur rin po che/ rin chen ngo bo gyur pa skye med bon gyi sgra/ skye med 
401.13(1)*: rig pa ya la zim/ gtod rnams ma go ma rtogs ma spyod rig pa'i ngo bor sangs 
401.14(1)*: rgyas shog/ 
401.15(1)*: gko dbye te/ shar gtod sku mdog dkar la gsal ba ni/ phyag na gsal byed 
401.16(1)*: 'phrul gyi lde mig bsdams/ gtod kyi nad rnams sel ba'i phyir/ bdag dang gya sbyor 
401.17(1)*: yon bdag gi/ nad rnams sel ba'i dngos grub gsol/ byang gtod skra mdog ldang 
401.18(1)*: la gsal ba ni/ phyag mtshan gsal ba'i lde mig bsdams/ gtod kyi nad rnams 
401.19(1)*: sel ba'i phyir/ bdag dang rgya sbyor yon bdag gi/ nad rnams sel ba'i dngos grub 
401.20(1)*: gsol/ nub gtod skra mdog dmar la gsal ba ni/ phyag mtshan gsal ba'i lje 
401.21(1)*: mig bsdams/ gtod kyi nad rnams sel ba'i phyir/ bdag dang rgya sbyor yon bdag 
402.1(1)*: la/ nad rnams sel ba'i dngos grub gsol/ lho gtod sku mdog ser la gsal ba 
402.2(1)*: ni/ phyag mtshan gsal ba'i lde mig bsdams/ gtod kyi rgyal po du nga ru dbu mang ni/ 
402.3(1)*: bdag dang rgyu sbyor yon bdag gi/ nad rnams sel ba'i dngos grub gsol/ 
402.4(1)*: bkra shis/ me bkra shis lha yi nhyi ma la/ gtod kyi rgyal po dung cu dbu mang 
402.5(1)*: ni/ bdag dang gya sbyor yon bdag la/ dbus kyi phyogs su bkra shis shog/ shar gyi 
402.6(1)*: phyogs su bkra shis pa/ shar phyogs dunga ri dkar po la/ bdag dang rgya sbyor yon 
402.7(1)*: bdag la/ shar gyi phyogs su bkra shis shog/ byang gi phyogs su bkra shis pa/ byang ri 
402.8(1)*: g.yu ri sngon po la/ bdag dang rgyu sbyor yon bdag la/ byang gi phyogs su bkra shis 
402.9(1)*: shog/ nub kyi phyogs su bkra shis pa/ nub gtod skra mdog dmar la gsal/ nub 
402.10(1)*: kyi phyogs su bkra shis shog/ lho yi phyogs su bkra shis pa/ lto gtod sku mdog sngo la 
402.11(1)*: gsal/ lho yi phyogs su bkra shis shog/ mtshams bzhi'i phyogs su bkra shis pa/ ska 
402.12(1)*: mdog dkar ser dmar ljang rsngo/ mtshams bzhi'i phyogs su bkra shis shog/ gtod 
402.13(1)*: rigs sum brgya drug cu ni/ skra mdog so sor gsal ba ni/ gtod rigs rnams kyi 
402.14(1)*: bkra shis shog/ gtod rigs brgyad khri bzhi stong ni/ gtod 'bum khri khri stong stong 
402.15(1)*: rnams/ bdag dang rgya sbyor yon bdag la/ gtod rigs rnams kyi bkra shis shog/ 
402.16(1)*: bdag dang gya sbyor yon bdag la/ gtod rnams dngos grub stsol ba'i bkra shis 
402.17(1)*: shog/ tshe lo brgya thub pa'i bkra shis shog/ gtod nad mi tshugs pa'i bkra shis shog/ 
402.18(1)*: gshegs su gsol te/ e gtod rnams dbus kyi phyogs su bskyod de gshegs/ 
402.19(1)*: shar phyogs gtod rigs bsam mi khyab/ shar gyi phyogs su bskyod de gshegs/ byang 
402.20(1)*: phyogs gtod rigs bsam mi khyab/ byang gi phyogs su bskyod de gshegs/ nub 
402.21(1)*: phyogs gtod rigs bsam mi khyab/ nub kyi phyogs su bskyod de gshegs/ lho phyogs 
403.1(1)*: gtod rigs bsam mi khyab/ lho yi phyogs su bskyod de gshegs/ 'og gi sa gtod 
403.2(1)*: bsam mi khyab/ 'og gi phyogs su bskyod de gshegs/ mtshams bzhi'i gtod rnams 
403.3(1)*: bsam mi khyab/ mtshams bzhi'i phyogs su bskyod de gshegs/ gtod rigs sum 
403.4(1)*: brgya drug cu dang / pha bong ri rab dag la gshegs/ rtsi shing nags tshal dag la 
403.5(1)*: gshegs/ so sor rang rang gnas su bskyod de gshegs/ gtod 'bum tshar ro// 
403.6(1)*: dpar byang smon tshig/ rnam gsum rgyal ba'i bstan pa gang / 'dzin skyong spel 
403.7(1)*: ba'i skyes mchog nyid/ dad gus ral pa'i rtser bkur nas/ yid rang sems kyi 
403.8(1)*: mchod sbrin 'bul/ rgyal ba'i zhal rlangs ma yal ba'i/ sgo bzhi mdzod lnga'i gsung 
403.9(1)*: gi tshogs/ 'phrul chen yi ge'i gzugs ris can/ snyigs lnga'i yang snyigs 'dir 
403.10(1)*: bzhugs mad/ las nyon dug gis bskran pa yi/ bzod med sdug bsngal skem pa 
403.11(1)*: dang / phan bde'i lang tsho bzhad pa'i gnyen/ gsung rab nyhi 'od 'di kho na/ bka' 
403.12(1)*: lung 'od snang mi ldan na/ 'dzam gling mun pas g.yog dang ltan/ mi rnams 'tsha
403.13(1)*: ba don dben byir/ bstan 'gro'i bsod nams gso ba'i slad/ ri dbang bzhin gyi 
403.14(1)*: snying stobs dang / lhag bsam dung gi dbu khyad 'og/ 'bri bzhengs dpar ba'i lam 
403.15(1)*: bzang nas/ rgyal gsung phyogs kun spel 'di bzang / 'khrul bral lung gi me long 
403.16(1)*: las/ sems can don du gsungs pa yi/ gsung rab 'bum sde khri sde 'di/ bdag 
403.17(1)*: gis ji ltar gsungs pa bzhin/ 'khrul pas lhag chad nor med par/ dung shog 
403.18(1)*: dakar la bris dag nas/ 'phrul gyi yi ge mkhan rnams dang / mtha' yas sems 
403.19(1)*: can gang rtsom pa/ bla med go 'phang gdon mi za/ zhes pa'i bsku med g.yung drung 
403.20(1)*: gsung / sting du sems pa'i nges shes las/ 'phrin las g.yel med skyong mdzad pa'i 
403.21(1)*: mchog sbrul 'od zer sbyin pa gtsos/ dag zhus yig bstar bris mkhan dang / lhag 
404.1(1)*: sems nus shugs mnyam brel dang / las don byed po thams cad dang / bsod 
404.2(1)*: nams tshogs gyi snying po che/ sgyu ma'i nor las len pa dang / rig gzhung tshe srog 
404.3(1)*: skyob pa'i ched/ dngos po'i mthun rkyen gtong phod pa'i/ 'byor ldan yon gyi bdag 
404.4(1)*: bcas la/ legs gsol yid rang phul tsam gyis/ dge ba'i skal pa mnyam 'gyur 
404.5(1)*: na/ stying nas mngon par bstod dang lhan/ gsung gi 'phrin las spel ba yi/ rla bs 
404.6(1)*: chen dge ba'i rtsa ba 'dis/ bla slob yon bdag bcas pa yi/ bar chod kyen ngan 
404.7(1)*: mthar bcil nas/ bsam don lhun gyis 'grub pa dang / mthar yang gdod ma'i 
404.8(1)*: zhing khams su/ bdag gzhan don gnyis byang chub nas/ chabs cig mngon sangs 
404.9(1)*: rgyas par shog/ lung rtogs bstan pa'i snying po gang / srid pa'i mthar yang gnas 
404.10(1)*: pa dang / ris med bstan 'dzin skyes bu'i tshogs/ 'gro don gegs med lhun grub 
404.11(1)*: shog/ yangs pa'i zhing khams thams cad du/ nad mtshon mu ge rgyan chad nas/ 'gro 
404.12(1)*: rnams zhi bde'i dpal yon la/ longs su spyod pa'i bkra shis shog/ ces pa'i 'bol 
404.13(1)*: csom smon tshig 'di nyid g.yung drung bon gyi gdan sa dpal ldan khri brtan nor bu'i 
404.14(1)*: rtse nas slob dpon gyi ming 'dzin tshangs pa bstan 'dzin 'bod pas '1
404.15(1)*: nyin bris te phul ba'o// 
404.16(1)*: brtan 'dzin rkyes mchag 'od zer sbyin pa yis 
404.17(1)*: bstan skyong lha mi gshen dang dpung spel te/ 
404.18(1)*: bstan pa'i snying po sgo bzhi mdzod lnga'i bon/ 
404.19(1)*: bstan 'gro'i dpal du bstun 'di rtag brtan 
405.1(1)*: sko bzhi mdzad dang lnga yi bon 
405.2(1)*: sa yi rdul ltar rgyas 'phel nas/ 
405.3(1)*: rin chen sna lnga'i gter bzhin du/ 
405.4(1)*: sems can don du rgyas par shog/ 
405.5(1)*: zhus bsgrigs tshan pa'i gsal bshad/ gong gsal ma dpe ni/ dbal khyud 
405.6(1)*: dgon pa'i bka' 'gyur gras su yod pa'i lag bris yig nag 'phrul dpar can 
405.7(1)*: byas pa yin/ dpe rgyan gzhan pa'i bskur ya ma rnyed pas zhus pos mthong tshod kyis 
405.8(1)*: bris pa'i chad lhag dang / mngon gsal can gyi skyon cha zon rigs kha bskangs byas 
405.9(1)*: na'ang / ma dpe la gang byung gis btcos thal ma byas/ da dun dpon gsas khyan 
405.10(1)*: rgod kyi nye lam sde bzhi'i gras su yod pa'i gtod 'bum le'u chung de'ang 'dir sbam 
405.11(1)*: bsgrigs byas te/ gsung rab sgo mdzod rin po che'i glegs bam re gyi de ba grangs 
405.12(1)*: 16nang zhus bsgrigs byas yod kyang da dung ma rtogs dbang gis tchad lhag 
405.13(1)*: sogs yod nges te/ spyi lo/ 6yar sngon lo ngo lnga brgya lhag nas gangs can bod 
405.14(1)*: kyi yul du yi ge'i par khang 'dzugs bspyan dang / dpe gzhi legs bsgrigs byas 
405.15(1)*: pa'i 'grems srel yongs khyab byed srol dar zin na'ang / g.yung drung bon gyi dpe 
405.16(1)*: gzhi'i bsdu bsgrigs byed pa'i go skabs kyi khor yug de tsam byung med pas/ 'dir 
405.17(1)*: phyogs la nyams myong dang lag len sogs la mig ltos len gzhi d kon pas gom 
405.18(1)*: kha gsar du yin pa dang / sgos su nged zhus bsgrigs pa tsho yang mkhyen dpyod rab 
405.19(1)*: 'byams pa min khar/ 'di'i zad mthun kyen nyung la 'gal rkyen mang ba'i gseb 
405.20(1)*: tu da la brmling 'grig po rang ma byung na/ phyogs gang sa'i khor yug dang gnas 
406.1(1)*: stangs tshad las brgal ba'i legs cha zhig zon thabs med pas/ de lugs kyis 
406.2(1)*: rjes su gzigs mkhan rnam pas 'di la dge skyon zad yo bsrang yong nges gnang 
406.3(1)*: re che zhing / 'di yi byas pa 'dis kyang slad du g.yung drung bon gyi lung gi bstan pa 
406.4(1)*: rin po che gsal dag 'grig po'i zhabs zhu'i grabs bsdogs tsam du 'gyur snyam che

406.6(1)*: nyin/ spyi lo '12nyin/ 
406.7(1)*: khyab po steng chen dgon sgo mdzod dpe zhus tshan pas/
